        (function() {
          var errorQueue = [];
          var newRelicReady = false;

          function flushErrorQueue() {
            if (window.newrelic && errorQueue.length > 0) {
              newRelicReady = true;
              const buildTag = document.body.dataset.buildTag || '';
              const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location?.search || '');
              // Normalize param keys to lowercase
              const normalized = {};
              for (const [key, value] of params.entries()) {
                normalized[key.toLowerCase()] = value;
              }

              const cellcode = normalized["cell"] ?? null;
              const icellcode = normalized["icell"] ?? null;
              window.newrelic.setCustomAttribute('Cell', cellcode || '');
              window.newrelic.setCustomAttribute('ICell', icellcode || '');
              window.newrelic.setCustomAttribute('BuildTag', buildTag);
              if (buildTag) window.newrelic.addRelease("creditcards", buildTag);
            }
            if (window.newrelic && errorQueue.length > 0) {
              while (errorQueue.length > 0) {
                var errorData = errorQueue.shift();
                window.newrelic.noticeError('ResourceLoadError', errorData);
              }
            }
          }

          function handleResourceError(element) {
            var tagName = element.tagName.toLowerCase();
            var resourceUrl = element.src || element.href || 'unknown';
            var isCrossOrigin = !resourceUrl.startsWith(window.location.origin);

            var urlParams = {};
            try {
              if (resourceUrl !== 'unknown') {
                var url = new URL(resourceUrl, window.location.origin);
                url.searchParams.forEach(function(value, key) {
                  urlParams[key] = value;
                });
              }
            } catch (e) {
              // Invalid URL, skip parameter extraction
            }

            var errorData = {
              errorType: tagName + 'LoadError',
              resourceType: tagName,
              failedResourceUrl: resourceUrl,
              pageUrl: window.location.href,
              crossOriginRequest: isCrossOrigin,
              urlParameters: urlParams
            };

            if (window.newrelic && newRelicReady) {
              window.newrelic.noticeError('ResourceLoadError', errorData);
            } else {
              errorQueue.push(errorData);
            }
          }

          // Check for New Relic periodically and flush queue
          var checkInterval = setInterval(function() {
            if (window.newrelic) {
              flushErrorQueue();
              clearInterval(checkInterval);
            }
          }, 100);

          // Stop checking after 5 seconds
          setTimeout(function() {
            clearInterval(checkInterval);
          }, 5000);

          var observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
            mutations.forEach(function(mutation) {
              mutation.addedNodes.forEach(function(node) {
                if (
                  (node.tagName === 'SCRIPT' && node.src) ||
                  (node.tagName === 'IMG' && node.src) ||
                  (node.tagName === 'LINK' && node.rel === 'stylesheet' && node.href)
                ) {
                  node.addEventListener('error', function() {
                    handleResourceError(this);
                  });
                }
              });
            });
          });

          if (document.documentElement) {
            observer.observe(document.documentElement, {
              childList: true,
              subtree: true
            });
          }
        })();

No Interest- just a fixed monthly fee<sup class="dagger-link font-arial leading-[.9] font-semibold text-inherit underline underline-offset-[.2em] [&amp;_a]:text-inherit"><a target="_blank" data-event-element-clicked="true" data-event-element-type="LINK" data-event-location="BODY" data-event-position="5" data-event-action-outcome="internalLink" data-event-custom-dimensions="componentVersion|1,componentName|RewardsBenefits" data-event-component-version="1" class="chaseanalytics-track-link text-inherit" href="https://sites.chase.com/services/creatives/pricingandterms.html/content/dam/pricingandterms/LGC61729.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-pt-name="cc_card_rbnfts_dagger">†</a></sup><sup> </sup>with plan durations that range from 3-24 months. You will be able to view Chase Pay Over Time plan options (including the fixed APR and durations) at checkout.</p><p><b>Keep in mind:</b> Even though you may have an eligible card, access to Chase Pay Over Time is not guaranteed.
